    Version 5.9

    Released Date:17-Jan-2015

    Changes in Manage Order Form,Limitation Form and ETA in each section of MO

    PCD:

    1.PCD date calculations have now been formulated so as to show a PRECISE PCD date, which all NEED TO FOLLOW.

    -: Ex-factory date change which may be a result of DC date change

    -: Bulk-In-House target change (delay beyond system target).

    ORDER LIMITATION FORM:

    1.This section now removes the requirement of the production department to provide any limitation or sign. Merchandising, Fabric & Accessory Dept. to continue this procedure.

    2.Fabric department - The Bulk ETA is a logical calculated date which is derived from the date of the order and the date of ex-factory/PCD.

    3.The number of days from order date (fabric lead time) till Bulk ETA shall be shown in a box below each fabric.

    4.Fabric department can change this date in view of their supplier limitation, however if this number (of days) increases, this will impact the costed CMT (this change shall be seen on the upcoming release 5.10) and also push the PCD closer to the ex-factory date, which has a negative impact on production days available vis-a-vis the ex-factory, maybe requiring an increase in the lines and/or increasing OB workstations also, which will increase the CMT and cause losses in production.

    Manage Orders (M.O.):

    1.The look of the M.O. has changed essentially with below changes and by reducing white spaces to optimise the view to a comfort screen-fit for easy and complete view

    2.Basic Info Section:“Buyer PO Pending” is seen towards the bottom of this section in red, till such time the Merchandiser does not upload the buyer’s P.O (from order form). This is an FYI information only and once P.O. is uploaded this comment shall vanish.

    -: PP Meeting form link is now available in this section by clicking the Serial number (along with the order form, fabric order form etc., at bottom of existing list)..

    3.FABRIC SECTION: The fabric section has changes in the look.

    -: New inclusions : Start ETA of Bulk and End ETA of bulk are 2 new date fields included next to each fabric for inputting latest information on the fabric to be received - this is an important and compulsory entry.

    -: Upon entering the final meterage count (100% or more) the date of such entry will automatically show next to the percentage to show the date of fabric completion

    4.ACCESSORY SECTION: The accessory section has changes in the look.

    -: Similar to the fabric section the user is required to input an ETA against each accessory, however there is only one ETA required in this section, which is the End ETA. This is an important and compulsory entry

    -:Upon entering the final meterage or count (100% or more) the date of this entry will automatically show next to the percentage

    5.TECHNICL SECTION: This section has various and important changes in the look as well as functionality.

    -: This comprises of 2 sub-sections:

    -: TECHNICAL (PROD):

    -: PCD date is now system calculated based on SAM/OB/available minutes and is hence PRECISE. This date needs to be respected and honoured by all departments

    -: SAM: The latest SAM value can be viewed here, be it the Costing SAM or the Production SAM, it will be shown with the correct narrative.

    -: OB: Similarly the latest OB count can be viewed here, be it the Costing OB or the Production OB, it will be shown with the correct narrative.

    -: OB file: The blue hyperlink next to the OB shall be clickable, and here one can view the latest OB file (whether Costing or Production - whichever has been entered latest).

    -: Available minutes : The available minutes (in lakhs) to produce the particular contract (not complete Style) is calculated to precision and shown next to the OB.

    -: Lines : The number of lines required to produce the ENTIRE STYLE (not just the viewed contract) is calculated and shown here, this is also quite optimised to the nearest count.

    -: The difference between the ex-factory date and the PCD date is set at 7 days, which essentially takes care of the time for cutting and finishing / packing to achieve the ex-factory date.

    -: For STC, Graded, Pattern/Sample and TOP, a driven target date is initially provided for every new order based on PCD date and the user needs to replace with correct ETA’s from time to time

    -: This is to be entered via a pop-up box for each field, which will show all contracts on the style, and also allow user to feed their remarks.

    -: User needs to enter ETA’s for Cutting Sheet and Production file (no system driven entry - blank) - however these are through a calendar entry and no pop-up is available/required for remarks.

    -: The QA status pop-up box does NOT exist any longer as it was redundant.

    6. PRODUCTION SECTION: The look of this section has also changed and sections re-aligned.

    -: The ex-factory date and the mode is now shown at the top.

    -: This is now THE FINAL FINAL ex-factory date with ZERO BUFFER. We all need to ensure this date is met as no extensions/manipulations possible (penalty starts after this date).

    -: The background colour (green, orange, red) of this section has now been removed. However, in case the FINAL ex-factory is missed, this section with go RED.

    -: The production section consisting of:'cut' which requires only the cut start date to be entered (this is part of release 5.10) and shall presently show a blank field (deemed to be same as PCD date) .

    -: cut ready requires 2 entries - cut ready start ETA and cut ready end ETA.

    -: Stitch also requires 2 entries - stitch start ETA and stitch end ETA.

    -: Similarly V.A. also requires 2 entries - V.A. start ETA and V.A. end ETA - THIS SECTION REQUIRES AN ENTRY FOR ALL VALUE ADDITIONS LIKE ADDA, HAND EMB. GARMENT PRINTING, WASHING ETC.

    -: packed requires just 1 entry which is the end ETA of packing.

    -: Just below this section is the shipment offer date which is entered by the production department in their regular production planning file and is also viewed here.

    Attendant Name: Anu Dayal,Raj,Mr Vinay,Mr Tej,Mr Raman

    2.Cut Avg once filled on MO, will be rolled back on the fabric order form and the costing sheet. The person filling the cut avg will have the option to update cut average for single contract or all contracts for this style number + fabric quality + print/color combo.

    3.Fabric order form will get roll back of cut average and new quantities required by cutting will be updated. It will create a task on dashboard, in case cut average is less or more than the fabric ordered average. This helps the fabric dept to control the order qty with the supplier and see what can be done to increase/reduce.

    4.Costing form will get roll back of cut average and also the correct fabric quality name and color/print. Any reduction or increase in fabric expense will be adjusted with the profit margin and an acknowledge task will be created for sales manager to click. This is similar to the earlier release where change in SAM or OB reflects on the CMT and any changes are adjusted with the profit margin on the cost sheet. This will help us in analysing post shipment costings and understand what styles are suitable to us over a period of time

    Attendant Name:Anu Dayal,Raj,Mr Vinay,Mr Tej,Mr Raman

    Version 5.2

    1. Sales Report: - User (authentic user) can view sales client report on the basis of Ex-Factory/Order Date/DC Date. The figures in report quantity is in Thousands, BIPL revenue is in Crore and ikandi revenue is in Millions. The report is available monthly + weekly bases, as a week consider Monday to Saturday. A new functionality also amended if a user selects a week in a report and click SUBMIT then automatically the data will be filter on Manage Order

    2. Manage Order: - New filters are available on Manage Order i.e. Data filtered base (Ex- Factory, DC and Order Date), Year base and Week base. These filters work on these three combinations eg. If user wants data whose Ex-Factory is in January’s first week of 2015. Then user need to select “Data Filtered” as Ex-Factory, “Year” as 2015 and “Week” as from 1(1-4 Jan) To 1(1-4 Jan). So similarly its works for DC date and Order Date too. These filters are mandatory and user need to take care when they are searching any style/order

    3. Allocation Form: - Now the allocation does not confirmed by final submit of form whereas as soon as the user allocate the unit against any contract, then unit is allocated. After the unit is allocated then the data will not be available for that contract in that form

    4. Shipment Remarks: - Issue related to $ sign in shipment Remarks is resolved

    5. Currency Admin:- Conversion rate updation can be done on the basis of already existing costing (whose status is less than or equally to Costing BIPL) or Quoted costing.
